○001503○se_gaya
●001503●se_gaya

○001504○When I picked up my tray, I found that it really was an appropriately breakfasty choice.

○001506○Save him a rice ball
●001506●给他揉一个饭团

●001507●给他带点秋刀鱼上的日本柑橘

○001508○Save him the fermented soybeans
●001508●给他带点纳豆

○001509○selbtn : 
●001509●selbtn : 

○001510○After finishing off the side dishes I flipped over the rice bowl, lightly dusted my hands with salt, and formed the rice into a ball. 
●001510●我把菜吃完了之后，将饭碗翻了过来，放在了手上并撒上了盐，做成了饭团。

○001511○I ate the grilled fish without using the half of a citrus fruit that came with it as a seasoning.
●001511●我在一点没碰上面的日本柑橘的情况下，把秋刀鱼吃完了。（注：かぼす/カボス，注释集内有图，主要产于大分县，是一种外形类似柠檬的绿色柑橘。能使一些日本菜肴增味不少，尤其是在烤鱼和吃鱼片时。有说法称是在江户时代从中国引进日本，但译者并未找到相关记载）

○001512○The fermented soybeans came in a little styrofoam pack, so they were easy to carry. I ate everything except them.
●001512●纳豆是单独包装的，所以很容易携带。我把除此之外的东西全部吃完了。

○001513○I returned the tray and went back to our room.
●001513●我把托盘还了回去，回到了房间。

○003741○As she did so another lunchlady came around with a plate piled high with meat, bean sprouts, and sliced onions and peppers. She set it off to the side and layered the veggies on the griddle, finally adding the meat atop them.
●003741●然后另一位大妈把盛有肉，豆芽，洋葱和青椒的盘子放在了旁边，把蔬菜分层摆到了锅里，最后把肉放到了上面。

○003742○As she did that, the first lunchlady who'd brought the pan out returned again with a dish full of sauce, which she placed on the table as well.
●003742●然后搬锅的大妈回来了，把盛有调味汁的小盘子放到了桌子上。
